These files log visitors when they visit websites. All hosting companies do this and a part of hosting services' analytics. The information collected by log files include internet protocol (IP) addresses, browser type, Internet Service Provider (ISP), date and time stamp, referring/exit pages, and possibly the number of clicks. These are not linked to any information that is personally identifiable. The purpose of the information is for analyzing trends, administering the site, tracking users' movement on the website, and gathering demographic information. The information is used to optimize the users' experience by customizing our web page content based on visitors' browser type and/or other information.</p> <p data-v-0a5fe658="">For more general information on cookies, please read <a data-v-0a5fe658="" href="https://www.cookieconsent.com/what-are-cookies/">"What Are Cookies"</a>.</p> <h2 data-v-0a5fe658="">Advertising Partners Privacy Policies</h2> <p data-v-0a5fe658="">You may consult this list to find the Privacy Policy for each of the advertising partners of TaiAn Financial.</p> <p data-v-0a5fe658="">Third-party ad servers or ad networks uses technologies like cookies, JavaScript, or Web Beacons that are used in their respective advertisements and links that appear on TaiAn Financial, which are sent directly to users' browser. If you would like to exercise any of these rights, please contact us.</p> <h2 data-v-0a5fe658="">GDPR Data Protection Rights</h2> <p data-v-0a5fe658="">We would like to make sure you are fully aware of all of your data protection rights. Every user is entitled to the following:</p> <p data-v-0a5fe658="">The right to access – You have the right to request copies of your personal data. We may charge you a small fee for this service.</p> <p data-v-0a5fe658="">The right to rectification – You have the right to request that we correct any information you believe is inaccurate. You also have the right to request that we complete the information you believe is incomplete.</p> <p data-v-0a5fe658="">The right to erasure – You have the right to request that we erase your personal data, under certain conditions.</p> <p data-v-0a5fe658="">The right to restrict processing – You have the right to request that we restrict the processing of your personal data, under certain conditions.</p> <p data-v-0a5fe658="">The right to object to processing – You have the right to object to our processing of your personal data, under certain conditions.</p> <p data-v-0a5fe658="">The right to data portability – You have the right to request that we transfer the data that we have collected to another organization, or directly to you, under certain conditions.</p> <p data-v-0a5fe658="">If you make a request, we have one month to respond to you.
